to zom...@yahoogroups.com, zomi-marsha...@googlegroups.com
Ih minam a dingin, deihsakna leh kipumkhat na apiang sakzo ding penpen ah, Code nei nai lo a hih hanga ki guang thei ding a hih nak leh Zomi mah cih ding a hihi.
Ahi zongin, Code neinai lote kiguang theilo ding ongcih mawk uh leh bel thudang ngaihsun kawikawi nawnlo in, ZO code om namun  pen zatpah ding a hihi.
Zomi ih cih na pen ih minam min ih mang ngilh loh na dingin ih Pu I Pa te in Zomi hihang cih ihmangngilh loh na dingin onghilh uhi cih ih tel  theih ding thupi mahmah hi.
ZO = cihna pen Nammin hi a mihing leh ganhing kikhen nailo hi-in, leitung a om nakhat peuhpeuh te min ahihi.
MI = cihna pen Ganhing hilo mihing cih gentel na ( hilhcian na)  hi a,  amalgawm dante ihtel keimawk leh ih khangthak naupang te nakbuai pha mahmah ding uhi. 
Ihpau ihham kibatloh nahang a, ih kisap dan leh ih kilawh dan te kilamdang hibek a, amau pau leh amau aw suah tekin akhiat na te ngaihsun le hangin  aki lamdang kilkel lo minam min te:
ZOMI  / MIZO  / ZO  ci a kisaam ahih MI hing minam minte pen kikhen thei hilo in, paihding zong omtuan kilkel lo a, ahang pen pau ki batloh nahang bek ahih man in, Ei ih pau akihuang thei zawdeuh teng min dingin, Zomi or Zo cih khat zawzaw ihzat nak leh ih minam min ZOMI  or ZO cih ihnam min pen mangngeilo ding ahihi.
Hih Pu, Dam Khua Nang hong atkhiat  2014 Census thei ding  minnam sawm teng lak ah, Chin bek paihding om a, adang Minam min  kiguang namkua tengpen namkhat bek hi -in, Chin minam te lobuang a dangdang  9 minam khempeuh pen, ZOMI  or Zo = minamkhat laigui zomkhat  Tun sungkhatpan piang te vive hi hang.
Thang C Khai
      USA

akhiat na te ngaihsun le hangin  aki lamdang kilkel lo minam min te:\u003c/div\u003e\r\n\u003cdiv\u003e\u003cbr\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\u003cdiv\u003eZOMI  / MIZO  / ZO  ci a kisaam ahih MI hing minam minte pen kikhen thei hilo in, paihding zong omtuan kilkel lo a, ahang pen pau ki batloh nahang bek ahih man in, Ei ih pau akihuang thei zawdeuh teng min dingin, Zomi or Zo cih khat zawzaw ihzat nak leh ih minam min ZOMI  or ZO cih ihnam min pen mangngeilo ding ahihi.\u003c/div\u003e\r\n\u003cdiv\u003e\u003cbr\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\u003cdiv\u003eHih Pu, Dam Khua Nang hong atkhiat  2014 Census thei ding  minnam sawm teng lak ah, Chin bek paihding om a, adang Minam min  kiguang namkua tengpen namkhat bek hi -in, Chin minam te lobuang a dangdang  9 minam khempeuh pen, ZOMI  or Zo \u003d minamkhat laigui zomkhat  Tun sungkhatpan piang te vive hi hang.\u003c/div\u003e\r\n\u003cdiv\u003e\u003cbr\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\u003cdiv\u003e\u003cbr\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\u003cdiv\u003eThang C
